  </a>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice">\n    <!-- CentralNotice -->\n   </div>\n   <div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n   </div>\n   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">\n    Scientific research on the International Space Station\n   </h1>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">\n     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n    </div>\n    <div id="contentSub">\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">\n     Jump to:\n     <a href="#mw-head">\n      navigation\n     </a>\n     ,\n     <a href="#p-search">\n      search\n     </a>\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">\n     <div class="mw-parser-output">\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2002" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg/220px-ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg/330px-ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg/440px-ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ISS-08_Michael_Foale_conducts_an_inspection_of_the_Microgravity_Science_Glovebox.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Expedition_8" title="Expedition 8">\n          Expedition 8\n         </a>\n         Commander and Science Officer\n         <a href="/wiki/Michael_Foale" title="Michael Foale">\n          Michael Foale\n         </a>\n         conducts an inspection of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Microgravity_Science_Glovebox" title="Microgravity Science Glovebox">\n          Microgravity Science Glovebox\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:382009main_MELFI12.jpg">\n         <img alt="European Space Agency (ESA) astronaut Thomas Reiter, STS-116 mission specialist, works with the Passive Observatories for Experimental Microbial Systems in Micro-G (POEMS) payload in the Minus Eighty Degree Laboratory Freezer for ISS (MELFI) in the Destiny laboratory of the International Space Station while Space Shuttle Discovery was docked with the station. MELFI is a low temperature freezer facility with nominal operating temperatures of -80, -26 and +4 \xc2\xb0C that will preserve experiment materials over long periods." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3032" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/382009main_MELFI12.jpg/220px-382009main_MELFI12.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/382009main_MELFI12.jpg/330px-382009main_MELFI12.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/382009main_MELFI12.jpg/440px-382009main_MELFI12.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:382009main_MELFI12.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         ESA astronaut Thomas Reiter, STS-116 mission specialist, works with the Passive Observatories for Experimental Microbial Systems in Micro-G (POEMS) payload in the Minus Eighty Degree Laboratory Freezer for ISS (MELFI) inside the Destiny laboratory.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Scientific research on the\n        <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n         International Space Station\n        </a>\n       </b>\n       is a collection of experiments that require one or more of the unusual conditions present in\n       <a href="/wiki/Low_Earth_orbit" title="Low Earth orbit">\n        low Earth orbit\n       </a>\n       . The primary fields of research include\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zero_g#Health_effects_of_weightlessness" title="Zero g">\n        human research\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_medicine" title="Space medicine">\n        space medicine\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Life_science" title="Life science">\n        life sciences\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Physical_science" title="Physical science">\n        physical sciences\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Astronomy" title="Astronomy">\n        astronomy\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Meteorology" title="Meteorology">\n        meteorology\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ISS_overview_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ISS_overview-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_Fields_of_Research_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_Fields_of_Research-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_ISS_Goals_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_ISS_Goals-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA_Authorization_Act_of_2005" title="NASA Authorization Act of 2005">\n        2005 NASA Authorization Act\n       </a>\n       designated the American segment of the International Space Station as a national laboratory with the goal of increasing the use of the ISS by other federal agencies and the private sector.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Research on the ISS improves knowledge about the effects of long-term space exposure on the human body. Subjects currently under study include\n       <a href="/wiki/Muscle_atrophy" title="Muscle atrophy">\n        muscle atrophy\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Osteoporosis" title="Osteoporosis">\n        bone loss\n       </a>\n       , and fluid shift. The data will be used to determine whether\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_colonisation" title="Space colonisation">\n        space colonisation\n       </a>\n       and lengthy\n       <a href="/wiki/Human_spaceflight" title="Human spaceflight">\n        human spaceflight\n       </a>\n       are feasible. As of 2006, data on bone loss and muscular atrophy suggest that there would be a significant risk of fractures and movement problems if astronauts landed on a planet after a lengthy interplanetary cruise (such as the six-month journey time required to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manned_mission_to_Mars" title="Manned mission to Mars">\n        fly to Mars\n       </a>\n       ).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JCB_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JCB-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Large scale medical studies are conducted aboard the ISS via the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Space_Biomedical_Research_Institute" title="National Space Biomedical Research Institute">\n        National Space Biomedical Research Institute\n       </a>\n       (NSBRI). Prominent among these is the\n       <a href="/wiki/Advanced_Diagnostic_Ultrasound_in_Microgravity" title="Advanced Diagnostic Ultrasound in Microgravity">\n        Advanced Diagnostic Ultrasound in Microgravity\n       </a>\n       study in which astronauts (including former ISS Commanders\n       <a href="/wiki/Leroy_Chiao" title="Leroy Chiao">\n        Leroy Chiao\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Gennady_Padalka" title="Gennady Padalka">\n        Gennady Padalka\n       </a>\n       ) perform ultrasound scans under the guidance of remote experts. The study considers the diagnosis and treatment of medical conditions in space. Usually, there is no physician on board the ISS, and diagnosis of medical conditions is a challenge. It is anticipated that remotely guided ultrasound scans will have application on Earth in emergency and rural care situations where access to a trained physician is difficult.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Researchers are investigating the effect of the station\'s near-weightless environment on the evolution, development, growth and internal processes of plants and animals. In response to some of this data, NASA wants to investigate\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Microgravity" title="Microgravity">\n        microgravity\n       </a>\n       \'s effects on the growth of three-dimensional, human-like tissues, and the unusual protein crystals that can be formed in space.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_Fields_of_Research_2-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_Fields_of_Research-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The investigation of the physics of fluids in microgravity will allow researchers to model the behaviour of fluids better. Because fluids can be almost completely combined in microgravity, physicists investigate fluids that do not mix well on Earth. In addition, an examination of reactions that are slowed by low gravity and temperatures will give scientists a deeper understanding of\n       <a href="/wiki/Superconductivity" title="Superconductivity">\n        superconductivity\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_Fields_of_Research_2-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_Fields_of_Research-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The study of\n       <a href="/wiki/Materials_science" title="Materials science">\n        materials science\n       </a>\n       is an important ISS research activity, with the objective of reaping economic benefits through the improvement of techniques used on the ground.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other areas of interest include the effect of the low gravity environment on combustion, through the study of the efficiency of burning and control of emissions and pollutants. These findings may improve our knowledge about energy production, and lead to economic and environmental benefits. Future plans are for the researchers aboard the ISS to examine\n       <a href="/wiki/Aerosol" title="Aerosol">\n        aerosols\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ozone" title="Ozone">\n        ozone\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Water_vapor" title="Water vapor">\n        water vapour\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Oxide" title="Oxide">\n        oxides\n       </a>\n       in Earth\'s atmosphere, as well as\n       <a href="/wiki/Cosmic_ray" title="Cosmic ray">\n        cosmic rays\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cosmic_dust" title="Cosmic dust">\n        cosmic dust\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Antimatter" title="Antimatter">\n        antimatter\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Dark_matter" title="Dark matter">\n        dark matter\n       </a>\n       in the universe.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_Fields_of_Research_2-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_Fields_of_Research-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n  </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-18">\n         <a href="#NASA.27s_ISS_research_and_science_activity">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           NASA\'s ISS research and science activity\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-19">\n           <a href="#Human_research">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Human research\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-20">\n             <a [505]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other">\n        Other\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Scientific_research_on_the_International_Space_Station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Other">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       In May 2011,\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n        Space Shuttle Endeavour\n       </a>\n       mission\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-134" title="STS-134">\n        STS-134\n       </a>\n       carried 13\n       <a href="/wiki/Lego" title="Lego">\n        Lego\n       </a>\n       kits to the ISS, where astronauts built models and saw how they reacted in microgravity, as part of the Lego Bricks in Space program. The results were shared with schools as part of an educational project.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Banks_506-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Banks-506">\n         [506]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Eaton_507-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Eaton-507">\n         [507]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Planned:\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NICER" title="NICER">\n         NICER\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/OPALS" title="OPALS">\n         OPALS\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Scientific_research_on_the_International_Space_Station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: References">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 25em; -webkit-column-width: 25em; column-width: 25em; list-style-type: decimal;">\n       <ol class="references">\n        <li id="cite_note-ISS_overview-1">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          <b>\n           <a href="#cite_ref-ISS_overview_1-0">\n            ^\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          <cite class="citation web">\n           <a class="external text" href="http://www.shuttlepresskit.com/ISS_OVR/index.htm" rel="nofollow">\n            "International Space Station Overview"\n           </a>\n           .
